	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ForceRange;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RampMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowDetailmin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowDetailmax;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _shadowrim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _shadowrimOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat14;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat14 = u_xlat2.x * 0.125 + u_xlat8;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat8);
    u_xlat2.y = u_xlat2.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat14 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.y = u_xlat16_3.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_3.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

#extension GL_EXT_shader_texture_lod : enable
#endif

uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowDetailmax;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _shadowrim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _shadowrimOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _RimEmissTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _RimShapeTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowDetail;
UNITY_LOCATION(8) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowDetail2;
UNITY_LOCATION(9) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowColor;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
bool u_xlatb2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec2 u_xlat10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
vec3 u_xlat14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
vec3 u_xlat17;
vec3 u_xlat18;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
float u_xlat41;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = abs(u_xlat16_4.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(u_xlat16_4.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat16_41 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6.x = min(max(u_xlat6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat18.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat41 = min(max(u_xlat41, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat41 = clamp(u_xlat41, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat41 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat6.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat41 = (-u_xlat6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = vec2(u_xlat41) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _EmisssionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emissive;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShift;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _shapeST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _faceshadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _FresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FresnelFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainPlayerPositionWS;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ForceRange;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RampMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowDetailmin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowDetailmax;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _shadowrim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _shadowrimOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.y = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _RimEmissTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(8) uniform mediump sampler2D _RimShapeTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(9) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowDetail;
UNITY_LOCATION(10) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowDetail2;
UNITY_LOCATION(11) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowColor;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
bool u_xlatb2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec2 u_xlat10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
vec3 u_xlat14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_14;
bool u_xlatb14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
vec3 u_xlat18;
vec3 u_xlat19;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
float u_xlat42;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat1, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb2;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb2) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = abs(u_xlat16_16.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_16.x = min(u_xlat16_16.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = log2(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat16_42 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat7.x;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat19.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = u_xlat42 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat19.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat7.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat19.xy = vec2(u_xlat42) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-u_xlat19.x);
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat19.x) + u_xlat19.y;
    u_xlat42 = float(1.0) / u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat2.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat42 = log2(u_xlat7.x);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat42 = exp2(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.y = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
bool u_xlatb2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_14;
bool u_xlatb14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
vec3 u_xlat18;
vec3 u_xlat19;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;

mediump float u_xlat16_42;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat1, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb2;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb2) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = abs(u_xlat16_16.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_16.x = min(u_xlat16_16.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = log2(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat16_42 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat7.x;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat19.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = u_xlat42 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat19.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat7.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat19.xy = vec2(u_xlat42) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-u_xlat19.x);
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat19.x) + u_xlat19.y;
    u_xlat42 = float(1.0) / u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat2.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat42 = log2(u_xlat7.x);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat42 = exp2(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_19.x = texture(_ShadowDetail2, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat42 * u_xlat16_19.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_19.xyz = texture(_ShadowColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_19.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_19.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = min(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = max(u_xlat16_5.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.x = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
    u_xlat6.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_4.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.y = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat1, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb2;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb2) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = abs(u_xlat16_16.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_16.x = min(u_xlat16_16.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = log2(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat16_42 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat7.x;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat19.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = u_xlat42 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat19.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat7.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat19.xy = vec2(u_xlat42) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-u_xlat19.x);
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat19.x) + u_xlat19.y;
    u_xlat42 = float(1.0) / u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat2.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat42 = log2(u_xlat7.x);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat42 = exp2(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_19.x = texture(_ShadowDetail2, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat42 * u_xlat16_19.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_19.xyz = texture(_ShadowColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_19.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_19.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = min(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = max(u_xlat16_5.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.x = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
    u_xlat6.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_4.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat18.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_40) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat7.xxx * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat7.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat19.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = min(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = max(u_xlat16_5.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6.x = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat10_1.w * u_xlat10_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
    u_xlat6.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);

    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_4.x;

    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat18.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat7.xxx * u_xlat19.xyz;

    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat19.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;

    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat14.x * u_xlat14.x;

    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat16_16.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_16.x * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat26;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_14.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;

    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);

    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);

    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;

    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);

    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat1.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat1, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb14 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb14 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlatb14 || u_xlatb2;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb2) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = abs(u_xlat16_16.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_16.x = min(u_xlat16_16.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = log2(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat16_42 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat7.x;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat19.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat19.x = u_xlat42 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * u_xlat19.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat7.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat19.xy = vec2(u_xlat42) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-u_xlat19.x);
    u_xlat42 = (-u_xlat19.x) + u_xlat19.y;
    u_xlat42 = float(1.0) / u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat2.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat42 = log2(u_xlat7.x);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat42 = exp2(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat42 = u_xlat42 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_19.x = texture(_ShadowDetail2, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat42 * u_xlat16_19.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_19.xyz = texture(_ShadowColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_19.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_19.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = min(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = max(u_xlat16_5.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.x = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
    u_xlat6.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_4.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat18.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_40) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat7.xxx * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat7.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat19.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_40)) + (-u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat14.x * u_xlat14.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_40 * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_28 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_28 = log2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_28 = exp2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat16_16.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_16.x * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat26;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx + (-u_xlat18.xyz);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xxx * u_xlat11.xyz + u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat38);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat38) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat38 = min(max(u_xlat38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat38 = clamp(u_xlat38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat14.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-u_xlat14.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat16_15.x + u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat26 / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = texture(_RimShapeTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_14.x + _RimlightScale;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_14.x + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat38 + (-u_xlat16_27);
    u_xlat16_27 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_39;

    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat18.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat10_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_40) + u_xlat10_1.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat7.xxx * u_xlat19.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat7.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat19.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_40)) + (-u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat14.x * u_xlat14.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_40 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_7 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat10_7.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_28 = log2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_28 = exp2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat16_16.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_16.x * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat26;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx + (-u_xlat18.xyz);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xxx * u_xlat11.xyz + u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat38);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat38) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat38 = clamp(u_xlat38, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat14.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-u_xlat14.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat16_15.x + u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat26 / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat10_14.x = texture2D(_RimShapeTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat10_14.x + _RimlightScale;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat10_14.x + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat38 + (-u_xlat16_27);
    u_xlat16_27 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_27 * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = clamp(u_xlat16_15.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_15.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_27 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_27 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat10_14.x = texture2D(_RimEmissTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_14.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat0.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat10.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat10_14.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat10.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat10_14.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;

    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;

    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;

    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat14.x * u_xlat14.x;

    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat14.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat16_3.x + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat26 / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = texture(_RimShapeTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;

    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_3.x * -2.0 + 3.0;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHTopColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MainlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _InvRim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _AddLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightDarkcolor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightLerp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightScale2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RimlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;

};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.y = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _RimEmissTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _RimShapeTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowDetail;
UNITY_LOCATION(8) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowDetail2;
UNITY_LOCATION(9) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShadowColor;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
bool u_xlatb2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec2 u_xlat10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
vec3 u_xlat14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_16;
vec3 u_xlat17;
vec3 u_xlat18;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
float u_xlat41;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = abs(u_xlat16_4.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(u_xlat16_4.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2.x = exp2(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat16_41 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6.x = min(max(u_xlat6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat18.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat41 = min(max(u_xlat41, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat41 = clamp(u_xlat41, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat41 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat6.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat41 = (-u_xlat6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = vec2(u_xlat41) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + (-u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat41 = (-u_xlat18.x) + u_xlat18.y;
    u_xlat41 = float(1.0) / u_xlat41;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat41;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat2.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat41 = log2(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat41 = exp2(u_xlat41);
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat41 = min(max(u_xlat41, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat41 = clamp(u_xlat41, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_18.x = texture(_ShadowDetail2, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat16_18.x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = texture(_ShadowColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_18.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;

    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = _actorscale * _ActorScaleAttribute;
    u_xlat0.x = in_POSITION0.x / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.y = u_xlat16_3.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_3.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.yw = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).zx;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = max(u_xlat2, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2 = inversesqrt(u_xlat2);
    u_xlat14.xyz = vec3(u_xlat2) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat2) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = abs(u_xlat16_4.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(u_xlat16_4.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat2 = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * _shadowrim;
    u_xlat2 = exp2(u_xlat2);
    u_xlat16_41 = texture(_ShadowDetail, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6.x = min(max(u_xlat6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat6.x;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat18.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat41 = min(max(u_xlat41, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat41 = clamp(u_xlat41, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.x = u_xlat41 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat18.x;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat6.x + _shadowrimOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2 = min(max(u_xlat2, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2 = clamp(u_xlat2, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat41 = (-u_xlat6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18.xy = vec2(u_xlat41) + vec2(_ShadowDetailmin, _ShadowDetailmax);
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 + (-u_xlat18.x);
    u_xlat41 = (-u_xlat18.x) + u_xlat18.y;
    u_xlat41 = float(1.0) / u_xlat41;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat41;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2 = min(max(u_xlat2, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2 = clamp(u_xlat2, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat2 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat2;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat41 = log2(u_xlat6.x);
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat41 = exp2(u_xlat41);
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat41 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat41 = min(max(u_xlat41, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat41 = clamp(u_xlat41, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_18.x = texture(_ShadowDetail2, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat41 * u_xlat16_18.x;
    u_xlat16_16 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat16_16;
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = texture(_ShadowColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat16_18.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_16) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = min(u_xlat16_7.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = max(u_xlat16_7.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat2 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat2 = inversesqrt(u_xlat2);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat2) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2 = min(max(u_xlat2, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2 = clamp(u_xlat2, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat2) * u_xlat2 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_1.w * u_xlat16_1.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat2 + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat2;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat2;
    u_xlat17.x = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat2 * u_xlat17.x;
    u_xlat2 = min(u_xlat2, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_39;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_39) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_39 = min(max(u_xlat16_39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_39 = clamp(u_xlat16_39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat17.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat17.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_40) + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat2) * u_xlat17.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat2 = u_xlat6.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot((-u_xlat14.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_40)) + (-u_xlat14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat14.x * u_xlat14.x;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_40 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_6 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_6.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_28 = log2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_28 = exp2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat26 = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _RampMap_ST.x + _RampMap_ST.z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat26;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) + (-u_xlat17.xyz);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat11.xyz + u_xlat17.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat5.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat38);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat38) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat38 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat38 = min(max(u_xlat38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat38 = clamp(u_xlat38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat14.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat14.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat26 * u_xlat16_3.x + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat26 / u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = texture(_RimShapeTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_14.x + _RimlightScale;
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_14.x + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_27 = (-u_xlat16_15.x) + u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat38 + (-u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_15.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat16_27 = (-u_xlat16_15.x) + u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat38 + (-u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_15.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_27;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_3.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_16 * u_xlat16_15.x + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat10_14.x = texture2D(_RimEmissTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_14.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat0.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat10.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat10_14.xyz = texture2D(_RampMap, u_xlat10.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_14.xyz * vec3(u_xlat2) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

vec4 u_xlat0;
